* This file contains SUA Types P, R, RMZ, TMZ, TSA, #
* TRA (shown as respective class) and Controlled Airspace   #
* class A, B, C and D below FL095.      #
* Airspaces with upper limit below 700 feet are excluded    #
* to avoid distraction in visual circuits and outlandings.  #
*             #
* Time ending with L is local time and with Z is UTC. #

*######### USER ASSUMES ALL RISK OF USE ####################
*                                                           #
* Notes:                                                    #
* 1) Lower limit of Dutch Mil TMA's A and C1 (class B)      #
* is raised from FL065 to FL095 from FRI 1700 to SUN 2359   #
* LT and during legal holidays (This does not apply to TMZ  #
* TMZ A, C, D North and E).         #
* 2) Some parts of Dutch airspace in this file have   #
* several classifications, the more restrictive of the  #
* classifications in such cases shall be used.    #
* 3) Operating hours of controlled military aerodromes, #
* designated MIL CTR and MIL TMA, are MON-FRI 0800-1645 #
* excl. legal holidays. Check NOTAM's for up-to-date  #
* operating hours. Outside these hours contact Dutch Mil    #
* INFO on 132.350 before entering airspace (RMZ).     #
* 4) Refer to NOTAM's for activation of Restricted and      #
* Danger area's and changes in vertical limits.       #
* 5) Temporary Reserved Airspace (TRA), Temporary       #
* Segregated Area (TSA), Cross Border Area's (CBA), #
* EHD 41, EHD 42, EHR 49, EHR3C, EHR 4E, RMZ North Sea, #
* CIV Low Flying Area's (GLV), Civil Simulated Forced,  #
* MIL Landing Area’s and EHRs only activated by NOTAM are   #
* not included in this file.        #
* 6) This file includes Gliding and VFR Area's. Contact     #
* local clubs for info about activation, procedures and   #
* limitations.            #
* 7) Transition Altitude in Amsterdam FIR is 3500 MSL   #
* for VFR traffic.          #
* 8) This file includes Aerodrome Traffic Zones (ATZ) as    #
* dangerous areas.          #
*             #
*###########################################################
*
*####### PROHIBITED AIRSPACE (P) ###########################
*
*###########################################################
* Definition: an airspace of defined dimensions, above the  #
* land areas or territorial waters of the Netherlands,      #
* within which the flight of aircraft is prohibited.    #
*             #
* This term is only used when the flight of civil aircraft  #
* within the designated airspace is not permitted at any  #
* time under any circumstances.       #
*###########################################################
*

DC 0.5

*####### RESTRICTED AIRSPACE (R) ###########################
*
*###########################################################
* Definition: an airspace of defined dimensions, above the  #
* land areas or territorial waters of the Netherlands,  #
* within which the flight of aircraft is restricted in  #
* accordance with certain specified conditions.   #
*             #
* This term is used whenever the flight of civil aircraft   #
* within the designated airspace is not absolutely    #
* prohibited but may be made only if specified conditions   #
* are complied with. Thus, prohibition of flight except at  #
* certain specified times leads to the designation of the   #
* airspace as a 'restricted area' as would prohibition      #
* except in certain meteorological conditions. Similarly,   #
* prohibition of flight unless special permission has been  #
* obtained, leads to the designation of a restricted area.  #
*###########################################################
*

*####### TEMPORARY RESERVED AREAS (TRA) ####################
*
*###########################################################
* Definition: a defined volume of airspace normally under   #
* the jurisdiction of one aviation authority and      #
* temporarily reserved, by common agreement, for the  #
* specific use by another aviation authority and through    #
* which other traffic may be allowed to transit, under  #
* ATC clearance.            #
*###########################################################
*

*####### TEMPORARY SEGREGATED AREAS (TSA) ##################
*
*###########################################################
* Definition: a defined volume of airspace normally under   #
* the jurisdiction of one aviation authority and      #
* temporarily segregated, by common agreement, for the  #
* exclusive use by another aviation authority and through   #
* which other traffic will not be allowed to transit.   #
*###########################################################
*

**####### RADIO MANDATORY ZONES (RMZ) ######################
*
*##########################################################
* RMZs are areas wherein the carriage and operation of    #
* radio equipment is mandatory. Before entering a RMZ an  #
* initial call shall be made by pilots on the appropriate #
* COM channel.                #
*##########################################################
*

*####### TRANSPONDER MANDATORY ZONES (TMZ) #################
*
*###########################################################
* TMZs are areas wherein an operational mode S SSR  #
* transponder is mandatory for all aircraft.    #
*             #
* The TMZs are active H24, unless otherwise indicated.      #
* CTRs (up to 3000 ft AMSL) are excluded from the TMZs.     #
*###########################################################

*## ATZ ####################################################
*
*###########################################################
* Definition: an airspace of defined dimensions       #
* established around an aerodrome for the protection of     #
* aerodrome traffic.          #
*             #
* Civil ATZ           #
* An ATZ has been established around the following civil    #
* aerodromes. The activities conducted at these aerodromes  #
* make it undesirable for other aircraft, not engaged in    #
* these activities, to penetrate or otherwise disturb the   #
* traffic pattern. In this case, the ATZ is primarily       #
* reserved for use by aircraft participating in the   #
* activities of the aerodrome. Overflying aircraft are  #
* strongly recommended to stay clear of the ATZ.    #
*###########################################################
